It waits for completion with a deadline, and if that times out, forces a hard shutdown.\n\nWhen start() runs, it takes the write lock to create fresh queues and a new softShutdown channel before launching the shard goroutines. This is used for tracking series across restarts/reloads. But I don't think this is related to the resharding issue.\n\nLet me take a step back and think about what could cause samples to get stuck (pendingSamples metric stays high with no progress).\n\nLooking at where pendingSamples is incremented/decremented:\n- Incremented in enqueue() when data is added to queue\n- Decremented in updateMetrics() after data is sent (or failed)\n\nSo if pendingSamples stays high, it means either:\n1. Data is being enqueued but not sent\n2. Or the metrics are not being updated correctly\n\nLooking at the code flow:\n1. Append() calls enqueue() - if successful, increments pendingSamples\n2. runShard() reads from batchQueue and calls sendBatch()\n3. sendBatch() calls sendSamples() or sendV2Samples()\n4. Those methods call sendSamplesWithBackoff() or similar\n5. After send completes (success or error), updateMetrics() decrements pendingSamples\n\nSo for pendingSamples to stay high, the send must not be completing. Or the batches are not being read from the queue.\n\nLet me look at what could prevent runShard() from reading batches...Actually, let me look at what happens when resharding causes a sample to be re-enqueued to the new shards. The sample was in a batch in the old shard queue. During stop(), FlushAndShutdown is called which closes the old queue. The batches are sent (or dropped if too much time passes).\n\nBut what if a sample is TRYING to be enqueued during the transition?\n\n1. Sample arrives at Append()2. Append() calls enqueue() which takes RLock3. enqueue() sees softShutdown is closed and returns false4. Append() retries with backoff5. \n\nMeanwhile, stop() and start() complete, and Append() retries enqueue() against the newly created softShutdown channel. The sample gets appended to the new queue and should be sent by the new runShard. But looking at the enqueue select statement more carefully—when softShutdown is closed, it returns false immediately. The issue is that the select statement has a case for the closed channel and a default case that tries to append to the queue.\n\nThere's a potential race condition here. If we're reading from softShutdown at the exact moment it's being created in start(), the timing could be problematic. Let me trace through the sequence: reshardLoop receives numShards and calls stop(), which closes softShutdown under a read lock. All pending enqueuers see the closed channel and return false, then backoff. The stop() function waits for all read locks to release before taking the write lock, flushing queues, and waiting for completion. Then start() is called, which takes the lock, creates new queues, and creates a new softShutdown channel.\n\nThe critical issue is that an enqueuer might have already captured a reference to the old softShutdown channel before start() creates the new one. When that enqueuer wakes from backoff and calls enqueue() again, it could still be trying to read from the closed channel instead of the new one. The select statement doesn't actually read a value—it just blocks until the channel is closed or the context is done.\n\nReading from a closed channel returns immediately with ok=false, and a select on a receive from a closed channel will always succeed. So if an enqueuer holds a reference to the old softShutdown, the select succeeds immediately and returns false, triggering a retry. On the next attempt, it might get the new channel, which should work correctly.\n\nBut I'm missing something simpler here. Let me focus on what could actually prevent runShard from completing a send—I need to look at the send methods more carefully.","signature":"EoUjCkYICxgCKkDHJtupy/r+VASLuODwNyk0cfR7ACEwa3oLXj6At99hYU0a0/PMd8F+iMzCVuyj6vgJAWa3XHCZ37pc0mcEdypIEgwkDq4VnG6SFnOUW1UaDH2ESU5YTzx8bk0c4iIwyfzMiQglp5AYBexOA45sQH4SjtqIXEWjOq9KMNZRToD6DEvDHL99LDw7HSuZxbg8KuwhMK+SdpdF6kEFlnDv8DDLPiHSHRQFtez8EhTrAy9t4+RG+P51brQdpGy9uu15toofCUfctmiuLbFoha4ShHeZJ7VyDp2EfHIfEeQvAGmt3ykdOHhrfOeD1+NGv1QNt0KyDYYMPxQhrsqjBhPDPX3aoxM2zTSgLurXkmok5XuRYVIqPa/lBli6EOqOv/UEpGFDMgW4sgA7NHz+YL1B0jezQkgZ8CD6qFRqId6YPVHrNpA0JHmbJ3C+EBotKdBo3TRDcDEGoChmdiyuzsUZiJT0YpjBm83RVH2a6godjMp+yz7jFXLIMSw1N5YpkiwnzXit2NMwNNd9yJmWiqaleoYdmCFku+TOaUw0iefvfxPk18BL4tX+Zju3pW78ksXC96RBsKcz7UpP9BdMy6/GzzbXu6jwx2GtKxgWm5j2FfD0fsxRiUMnj1Z84URaz6DqYklPxeSDUldyBKxDSOqo+EeRKrFEYPh/tW6cnBCQci41qgQpdZpCv2LUGhmcZCn+1/EaUj9caS85BtGMABT/7NSnUu+Y5umJwxH4eF5/JLqqyfoVTEmGtsW3K6rbB2GB7HJfp4v/Iig2p++Gtgngsb/9X8rlVRlwPluh4ifq9XLLB/RwpJFB9qpe+pfnhm9yCnChVGl3H6p+C72uXAbdbcVAzBJNUD/e4O9f3QCNb25ibDNCDDf/ejO+H7Z7KXW11yE8iidX0jImVAhUucEim4Sh8/eEOAwlFDtDrb7tL4lVt9UIJGXP1rC6Rdsj9Tl+nJUMaynzja1MuY/Ta/dpM6jN7OWRrYJmrVDgO0eM7Bflc7xQfLq3+v7GQo+aLqAulUf/kSRRo5v1GvaCi/XhQI2hruxXY4Ew2dJe3nyt/RVT35n+fSnYciTRqtoeKRAw9whNwkMaR2nahvukbQ4jsEVhp5K+AiFLPHVFs63m0ZHyicMsKOvhttN2Apqc121WhRQi6k2w84efrNG6dWdN6IL0SvlaORFsgF/IiTp4Cd/jRV2ECPbWtFEK6E/lNqxif1UJ3kI4iosfCGV8WQUAUjdKN5Zpw8mZB2f3aWm1MtQymyfVXA1PymFak99K1XI9Us7X1WgwDFDgTG8RlfQ1bpaK9EHrAdOdoueoX8vTNk+EN0y8aeyUYSVhyOIs1eWT3d22P3eAHyfgFoX7Y4qq8mPMaDulEffdj0NNYxPVWYLMSDmL+Z0Qd9nOWv3Sq1+BJPDLITKYET2oFczI7SFUCQld3Svla9gqHuWgouw4Cp8KCp78qr4fNTLfMK5oTjZms8jJbrq+txfjbUM6Erj21szyNyNtnG+/9pHWX0U3XBP9etd0kvRMMvKCe5OSxjRpdyKiKWN8/RAm0vg/DMVw9fOmjlSqTjgEki/ma9/2hhIts3rsMf4qLmvT5sZZ89eXVxzQL/GKt0Aw4b+M0Hszj9tit4ndiG7UIoF1AE5dJDhNDUCSE0kYdvA8ENGosOEbPj7k/w/09jsJ8qh4Dkz74GWygDRkW8OfxufbXkIEyubrPTwjehRq2+ac4yKnvKg25N0a6Y7/of3TIUxFE28s0ObfQgiVJuQNg/wtl4bcUlMXFH5uF73OieHC2R+ejHXEH8M54f1BKSYEqu0guLxhtAQ1h42ueqEHkC5TKockdbvCbo4wsMZHD3Ze9V7NGXv/iNHXF96fOpZpcMIKMrp259W7MC3G101/JFweT+m/L2BIKQL/aPVHam8kRsSEK3M0FSDRfHEVTxGjeGxWpTCSHXX/WfQFIwVxHQdQgcLGnAv When new shards are started, this counter is reset to zero instead of being properly reconciled, leaving `prometheus_remote_storage_samples_pending` metric in a stalled state showing samples that were actually lost.\n\n## Root Cause\n\n**Location:** `storage/remote/queue_manager.go`\n\n**Mechanism:** Three interacting functions create a window where samples are lost but metrics are not properly updated:\n\n### 1. Resharding Orchestration (`reshardLoop`, line 1184-1199)\n```go\nfunc (t *QueueManager) reshardLoop() {\n    defer t.wg.Done()\n    for {\n        select {\n        case numShards := <-t.reshardChan:\n            t.shards.stop()      // Line 1193: Wait for flush\n            t.shards.start(numShards)  // Line 1194: Start new shards\n```\n\nThe reshardLoop calls `stop()` to cleanly flush all queues before starting new shards.\n\n### 2. Incomplete Flush on Shutdown (`queue.FlushAndShutdown`, lines 1447-1455)\n```go\nfunc (q *queue) FlushAndShutdown(done <-chan struct{}) {\n    for q.tryEnqueueingBatch(done) {\n        time.Sleep(time.Second)  // Line 1449\n    }\n    q.batchMtx.Lock()\n    defer q.batchMtx.Unlock()\n    q.batch = nil              // Line 1453: DISCARDS PARTIAL BATCH\n    close(q.batchQueue)        // Line 1454\n}\n```\n\nThe `FlushAndShutdown()` method tries to enqueue the partial batch but will silently discard it if:\n- The `batchQueue` channel remains full (no receiver draining it)\n- Hard shutdown is triggered via `<-done` before the batch is sent\n\n### 3. Metric Counter Reset (`shards.start`, lines 1256-1258)\n```go\nfunc (s *shards) start(n int) {\n    s.mtx.Lock()\n    defer s.mtx.Unlock()\n    // ... create new queues ...\n    s.enqueuedSamples.Store(0)      // Line 1256: RESET, NOT DECREMENT\n    s.enqueuedExemplars.Store(0)    // Line 1257\n    s.enqueuedHistograms.Store(0)   // Line 1258\n```\n\nThe new shards reset the enqueued sample counters to zero without accounting for samples lost from old shards.\n\n## Evidence\n\n### Code References\n\n1. **Sample Enqueuing** (`queue_manager.go:1312-1340` - `enqueue()` function):\n   - Line 1326: `s.qm.metrics.pendingSamples.Inc()` - increments when sample queued\n   - Line 1315: `shard := uint64(ref) % uint64(len(s.queues))` - calculates destination shard\n\n2. **Metric Decrement on Send** (`queue_manager.go:1689` - `updateMetrics()` function):\n   ```go\n   s.qm.metrics.pendingSamples.Sub(float64(sampleCount))  // Only called on successful send\n   ```\n\n3. **Flush Attempt** (`queue_manager.go:1459-1476` - `tryEnqueueingBatch()`):\n   - Line 1462-1463: Returns false if batch is empty\n   - Line 1467-1468: Returns false if batch successfully enqueued\n   - Line 1469-1472: Returns false if hard shutdown signal received\n   - Line 1475: Returns true (needs retry) only if `batchQueue` is full\n\n4. **Hard Shutdown Timing** (`queue_manager.go:1286-1294` - `stop()` function):\n   ```go\n   select {\n   case <-s.done:\n       return\n   case <-time.After(s.qm.flushDeadline):  // Default: 1 minute\n   }\n   // Force an unclean shutdown.\n   s.hardShutdown()  // Cancels context, triggering runShard to exit\n   <-s.done\n   ```\n\n## Race Condition Scenario\n\n```\nTimeline:\n1. [updateShardsLoop] Detects need to reshard from 4→6 shards\n2. [updateShardsLoop] Sends desiredShards to reshardChan\n3. [reshardLoop] Receives from reshardChan, calls shards.stop()\n4. [stop] Closes softShutdown, causing all active enqueue() calls to fail and retry\n5. [stop] Takes Lock (waiting for all enqueue RLocks to release)\n6. [stop] Launches FlushAndShutdown goroutines for each queue\n7. [queue.FlushAndShutdown] Tries to send partial batch:\n   - If batchQueue is full: tryEnqueueingBatch returns true, sleeps 1 second\n   - Meanwhile, runShard might be stuck in sendBatch() (network latency, slow endpoint)\n   - batchQueue channel remains full\n8. [stop] Timeout of flushDeadline (default 1 minute) expires\n9. [stop] Calls s.hardShutdown() canceling context\n10. [runShard] Receives ctx.Done():\n    - Calculates droppedSamples = enqueuedSamples.Load()\n    - Subtracts from pendingSamples\n    - But enqueuedSamples already reflects OLD samples plus NEW samples enqueued during transition\n11. [stop] Returns\n12. [reshardLoop] Calls shards.start()\n13. [start] Resets enqueuedSamples.Store(0) - LOSES ACCOUNTING OF LOST SAMPLES\n14. [start] Creates new empty shards\n15. New samples arrive and get queued\n    - But pendingSamples metric is now inconsistent with actual queued data\n```\n\n## Intermittency Analysis\n\nThe issue is **intermittent** because it depends on timing:\n\n1. **Condition A - Flush Timeout**: The hard shutdown must trigger (flushDeadline expires) rather than completing gracefully. This happens when:\n   - Remote endpoint is slow/unresponsive\n   - Network congestion during send attempts\n   - batchQueue remains full because runShard can't drain it fast enough\n\n2. **Condition B - Concurrent Traffic**: New samples must arrive during the transition window. If target discovery changes (adds/removes targets) and generates many new samples during resharding, enqueuers are blocked by softShutdown being closed, increasing the chance of partial batches being discarded.\n\n3. **Condition C - Partial Batch Exists**: A partial batch must exist (not yet full) at the moment resharding is initiated.\n\nAll three conditions must align for the metric to stall.\n\n## Affected Components\n\n- **`storage/remote/queue_manager.go`**:\n  - `QueueManager.reshardLoop()` - orchestrates reshard cycle\n  - `shards.stop()` - manages graceful shutdown with timeout\n  - `shards.start()` - initializes new shards, RESETS counters\n  - `queue.FlushAndShutdown()` - incomplete batch handling\n  - `shards.enqueue()` - adds to pendingSamples counter\n\n- **Metrics**:\n  - `prometheus_remote_storage_samples_pending` - stalled reporting\n  - `prometheus_remote_storage_pendingSamples` - internal counter (may show overflow)\n\n## Recommendation\n\n### Root Fix Strategy\n\nThe core issue is that `shards.start()` uses `.Store(0)` to reset the enqueued sample counters instead of decrementing them:\n\n```go\n// CURRENT (WRONG):\ns.enqueuedSamples.Store(0)\n\n// SHOULD BE:\noldSamples := s.enqueuedSamples.Load()\nif oldSamples > 0 {\n    s.qm.metrics.pendingSamples.Sub(float64(oldSamples))\n}\ns.enqueuedSamples.Store(0)\n```\n\nAdditionally, `queue.FlushAndShutdown()` should guarantee sending the partial batch or explicitly dropping it while updating metrics:\n\n```go\n// After the flush retry loop, if batch still exists:\nif len(q.batch) > 0 {\n    // Log dropped samples\n    s.qm.metrics.pendingSamples.Sub(float64(len(q.batch)))\n    s.enqueuedSamples.Sub(int64(len(q.batch)))\n}\nq.batch = nil\n```\n\n### Diagnostic Steps\n\n1. **Enable debug logging** for reshard operations:\n   ```\n   Storage/remote: set log level to DEBUG\n   Watch for: \"Resharding queues\" and \"Resharding done\" messages\n   Check timing between resharding start and completion\n   ```\n\n2. **Monitor these metrics during target discovery changes**:\n   ```\n   prometheus_remote_storage_samples_pending  # Should return to 0 after reshard\n   prometheus_remote_storage_shards           # Verify shard count changed\n   prometheus_remote_storage_sent_bytes_total # Should increase continuously\n   prometheus_remote_storage_failed_samples_total  # Watch for drops\n   ```\n\n3. **Confirm the diagnosis**:\n   - Track `pendingSamples` before resharding\n   - Observe if it stops decreasing after \"Resharding done\"\n   - Check if `failed_samples_total` increases (should be logged if >0 samples dropped)\n   - Compare `sent_bytes_total` rate before/after reshard (should remain steady)\n\n4. **Network/Endpoint health**:\n   - During resharding, monitor remote endpoint response times\n   - Check if endpoint becomes unavailable briefly\n   - Review `prometheus_remote_storage_slow_requests` (if available)\n   - Slow endpoint triggers timeout → hard shutdown → metric loss\n\n## Additional Notes\n\n- The default `flushDeadline` is typically 1 minute (configurable)\n- If resharding happens frequently with high throughput, probability of partial batch loss increases\n- The issue correlates with target discovery changes because they trigger resharding AND may generate sample spikes\n- Samples aren't actually lost from remote storage if they were already sent before the reshard; only in-flight/queued samples are affected\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":2,"cache_creation_input_tokens":2101,"cache_read_input_tokens":60128,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":2101},"output_tokens":2,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"5de4c864-e91e-4178-86a9-07b3ced0b230","uuid":"ccba7e54-770a-4984-82d1-2bdd17b7e0c0"}
